NBC ended the experiment after the 1987-88 season due to the low ratings put up by three of the series, with Out of This World being one of the two that was renewed. After its first season the series was largely moved to weekend time slots, where it remained until its cancellation following the fourth season.", "poster_path": "/bUT4VPKzb6qddIN9sc5ewsREKyq.jpg", "media_type": "tv", "adult": false, "original_language": "en", "genre_ids": [10765, 35, 10762], "popularity": 26.6845, "first_air_date": "1987-09-17", "vote_average": 7.3, "vote_count": 22, "origin_country": ["US"]}, {"backdrop_path": null, "id": 4102, "name": "Madame's Place", "original_name": "Madame's Place", "overview": "Madame's Place is an American sitcom that featured the misadventures of Madame, a puppet in the form of a bawdy old movie star with a naughty sense of humor.", "poster_path": "/mm3DIFaDVFAAFSTJtO3sosI918w.jpg", "media_type": "tv", "adult": false, "original_language": "en", "genre_ids": [], "popularity": 16.2742, "first_air_date": "1982-09-20", "vote_average": 7.3, "vote_count": 6, "origin_country": ["US"]}]}]}
